const int width = 1280;
const int height = 720;
int i;
float sudut;
double x_geser, y_geser, z_geser;

float pitch = 0.0, yaw = 0.0;
float camX = 0.0, camZ = 0.0, terbang = 25.0;

void display();
void reshape(int w, int h);
void timer(int);
void passive_motion(int, int);
void camera();
void keyboard(unsigned char key, int x, int y);
void keyboard_up(unsigned char key, int x, int y);

struct Motion {
    bool Forward, Backward, Left, Right, Naik, Turun;
};
Motion motion = { false,false,false,false,false,false };

void init() {
    glClearColor(0.529, 0.807, 0.921, 0.0);
    glutSetCursor(GLUT_CURSOR_NONE);
    glEnable(GL_DEPTH_TEST);
    glEnable(GL_BLEND);
    glBlendFunc(GL_SRC_ALPHA, GL_ONE_MINUS_SRC_ALPHA);
    glDepthFunc(GL_LEQUAL);
    glutWarpPointer(width / 2, height / 2);
}

void ground() {
    glBegin(GL_QUADS);
    glColor3f(0.21, 0.15, 0.03);
    glVertex3f(-1000.0, 0, -1000.0);

    glColor3f(0.21, 0.15, 0.03);
    glVertex3f(1000.0, 0, -1000.0);

    glColor3f(0.36, 0.3, 0.16);
    glVertex3f(1000.0, 0, 1000.0);

    glColor3f(0.21, 0.15, 0.03);
    glVertex3f(-1000.0, 0, 1000.0);
    glEnd();
}

void bangunan_lantai1() {
    // depan
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.95, 0.33, 0.06);
    glVertex3f(-300.0, 300.0, 100);
    glVertex3f(-300.0, 200.0, 100);
    glVertex3f(100.0, 200.0, 100);
    glVertex3f(100.0, 300.0, 100);
    glEnd();

    // belakang
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.95, 0.33, 0.06);
    glVertex3f(-300.0, 300.0, -300);
    glVertex3f(-300.0, 200.0, -300);
    glVertex3f(100.0, 200.0, -300);
    glVertex3f(100.0, 300.0, -300);
    glEnd();

    // atas
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.97, 0.97, 0.97);
    glVertex3f(-300.0, 300.0, -300);
    glVertex3f(-300.0, 300.0, 100);
    glVertex3f(100.0, 300.0, 100);
    glVertex3f(100.0, 300.0, -300);
    glEnd();

    // kiri
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.95, 0.33, 0.06);
    glVertex3f(-300.0, 300.0, 100);
    glVertex3f(-300.0, 200.0, 100);
    glVertex3f(-300.0, 200.0, -300);
    glVertex3f(-300.0, 300.0, -300);
    glEnd();

    // kanan
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.95, 0.33, 0.06);
    glVertex3f(100.0, 300.0, 100);
    glVertex3f(100.0, 200.0, 100);
    glVertex3f(100.0, 200.0, -300);
    glVertex3f(100.0, 300.0, -300);
    glEnd();
}

void bangunan_lantai2() {
    // depan
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.94, 0.32, 0.05);
    glVertex3f(-200.0, 470.0, 0);
    glVertex3f(-200.0, 320.0, 0);
    glVertex3f(0, 320.0, 0);
    glVertex3f(0, 470.0, 0);
    glEnd();

    // belakang
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.94, 0.32, 0.05);
    glVertex3f(-200.0, 470.0, -200);
    glVertex3f(-200.0, 320.0, -200);
    glVertex3f(0, 320.0, -200);
    glVertex3f(0, 470.0, -200);
    glEnd();

    // kiri
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.94, 0.32, 0.05);
    glVertex3f(-200.0, 470.0, -200);
    glVertex3f(-200.0, 320.0, -200);
    glVertex3f(-200.0, 320.0, 0);
    glVertex3f(-200.0, 470.0, 0);
    glEnd();

    // kanan
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.94, 0.32, 0.05);
    glVertex3f(0, 470.0, -200);
    glVertex3f(0, 320.0, -200);
    glVertex3f(0, 320.0, 0);
    glVertex3f(0, 470.0, 0);
    glEnd();
}

void atap_bawah1() {
    // depan
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.94, 0.32, 0.05);
    glVertex3f(-235.0, 490.0, 35);//titik kiri atas
    glVertex3f(-200.0, 470.0, 0);//titik kiri bawah
    glVertex3f(0.0, 470.0, 0);//titik kanan bawah
    glVertex3f(35, 490.0, 35);//titik kanan atas
    glEnd();

    // belakang
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.94, 0.32, 0.05);
    glVertex3f(-235.0, 490.0, -235);//titik kiri atas
    glVertex3f(-200.0, 470.0, -200);//titik kiri bawah
    glVertex3f(0.0, 470.0, -200);//titik kanan bawah
    glVertex3f(35, 490.0, -235);//titik kanan atas
    glEnd();

    // kiri
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.94, 0.32, 0.05);
    glVertex3f(-235.0, 490.0, -235);
    glVertex3f(-200.0, 470.0, -200);
    glVertex3f(-200.0, 470.0, 0);
    glVertex3f(-235.0, 490.0, 35);
    glEnd();

    // kanan
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.94, 0.32, 0.05);
    glVertex3f(35, 490.0, -235);
    glVertex3f(0.0, 470.0, -200);
    glVertex3f(0.0, 470.0, 0);
    glVertex3f(35, 490.0, 35);
    glEnd();
}

void atap_atas1() {
    // depan
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.3, 0.6, 0.62);
    glVertex3f(-200.0, 510.0, 0);//titik kiri atas
    glVertex3f(-350.0, 450.0, 150);//titik kiri bawah
    glVertex3f(155.0, 450.0, 150);//titik kanan bawah
    glVertex3f(5, 510.0, 0);//titik kanan atas
    glEnd();

    // belakang
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.3, 0.6, 0.62);
    glVertex3f(-200.0, 510.0, -200);//titik kiri atas
    glVertex3f(-350.0, 450.0, -350);//titik kiri bawah
    glVertex3f(155.0, 450.0, -350);//titik kanan bawah
    glVertex3f(5, 510.0, -200);//titik kanan atas
    glEnd();

    //atas
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.3, 0.6, 0.62);
    glVertex3f(-200.0, 510.0, -200);
    glVertex3f(-200.0, 510.0, 0);
    glVertex3f(5, 510.0, 0);
    glVertex3f(5, 510.0, -200);
    glEnd();

    // kiri
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.3, 0.6, 0.62);
    glVertex3f(-200.0, 510.0, -200);
    glVertex3f(-350.0, 450.0, -350);
    glVertex3f(-350.0, 450.0, 150);
    glVertex3f(-200.0, 510.0, 0);
    glEnd();

    // kanan
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.3, 0.6, 0.62);
    glVertex3f(5, 510.0, -200);
    glVertex3f(155.0, 450.0, -350);
    glVertex3f(155.0, 450.0, 150);
    glVertex3f(5, 510.0, 0);
    glEnd();
}

    glColor3f(0.86, 0.39, 0);
    glVertex3f(-350.0, 390, 150);// kiri atas

    glVertex3f(-325.0, 320, 150);// kanan bawah
    glVertex3f(-325.0, 390, 150);// kanan atas
    glEnd();

    //belakang
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.86, 0.39, 0);
    glVertex3f(-350.0, 390, 130);// kiri atas
    glVertex3f(-350.0, 320, 130);// kiri bawah
    glVertex3f(-325.0, 320, 130);// kanan bawah
    glVertex3f(-325.0, 390, 130);// kanan atas
    glEnd();

    //kiri
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.86, 0.39, 0);
    glVertex3f(-350.0, 390, 130);// kiri atas
    glVertex3f(-350.0, 320, 130);// kiri bawah
    glVertex3f(-350.0, 320, 150);// kanan bawah
    glVertex3f(-350.0, 390, 150);// kanan atas
    glEnd();

    //kanan
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.86, 0.39, 0);
    glVertex3f(-325.0, 390, 130);// kiri atas
    glVertex3f(-325.0, 320, 130);// kiri bawah
    glVertex3f(-325.0, 320, 150);// kanan bawah
    glVertex3f(-325.0, 390, 150);// kanan atas
    glEnd();
    glPopMatrix();

    // balok kanan
    glPushMatrix();
    glTranslatef(-95, 213.5, -90);
    //depan

void atap_bawah3() {
    // depan
    glPushMatrix();
    glTranslatef(0, 127.5, 0);
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.94, 0.32, 0.05);
    glVertex3f(-160.0, 680.0, -50);
    glVertex3f(-180.0, 695.0, -15);
    glVertex3f(-10, 695.0, -15);
    glVertex3f(-40, 680.0, -50);
    glEnd();

    // belakang
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.94, 0.32, 0.05);
    glVertex3f(-160.0, 680.0, -155);
    glVertex3f(-180.0, 695.0, -190);
    glVertex3f(-10, 695.0, -190);
    glVertex3f(-40, 680.0, -155);
    glEnd();

    //kiri
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.94, 0.32, 0.05);
    glVertex3f(-160.0, 680.0, -155);
    glVertex3f(-180.0, 695.0, -190);
    glVertex3f(-180.0, 695.0, -15);
    glVertex3f(-160.0, 680.0, -50);
    glEnd();

    //kanan
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.94, 0.32, 0.05);
    glVertex3f(-10, 695.0, -190);
    glVertex3f(-40, 680.0, -155);
    glVertex3f(-40, 680.0, -50);
    glVertex3f(-10, 695.0, -15);
    glEnd();
    glPopMatrix();
}

void atap_atas3() {
    // depan
    glPushMatrix();
    glTranslatef(0, 316, 0);
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.3, 0.6, 0.62);
    glVertex3f(-200.0, 550.0, 0);//titik kiri atas
    glVertex3f(-300.0, 480.0, 100);//titik kiri bawah
    glVertex3f(105.0, 480.0, 100);//titik kanan bawah
    glVertex3f(5, 550.0, 0);//titik kanan atas
    glEnd();

    // belakang
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.3, 0.6, 0.62);
    glVertex3f(-200.0, 550.0, -200);//titik kiri atas
    glVertex3f(-300.0, 480.0, -300);//titik kiri bawah
    glVertex3f(105.0, 480.0, -300);//titik kanan bawah
    glVertex3f(5, 550.0, -200);//titik kanan atas
    glEnd();

    //atas
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.3, 0.6, 0.62);
    glVertex3f(-200.0, 550.0, -200);
    glVertex3f(-200.0, 550.0, 0);
    glVertex3f(5, 550.0, 0);
    glVertex3f(5, 550.0, -200);
    glEnd();


    // kiri
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.3, 0.6, 0.62);
    glVertex3f(-200.0, 550.0, -200);
    glVertex3f(-300.0, 480.0, -300);
    glVertex3f(-300.0, 480.0, 100);
    glVertex3f(-200.0, 550.0, 0);
    glEnd();

    // kanan
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.3, 0.6, 0.62);
    glVertex3f(5, 550.0, -200);
    glVertex3f(105.0, 480.0, -300);
    glVertex3f(105.0, 480.0, 100);
    glVertex3f(5, 550.0, 0);
    glEnd();
    glPopMatrix();
}

void lancip() {
    //depan
    glPushMatrix();
    glTranslatef(0, 156.5, 0);
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.86, 0.9, 0.56);
    glVertex3f(-135, 730, -65);
    glVertex3f(-135, 710, -65);
    glVertex3f(-55, 710.0, -65);
    glVertex3f(-55, 730.0, -65);
    glEnd();

    //belakang
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.86, 0.9, 0.56);
    glVertex3f(-135, 730, -138);
    glVertex3f(-135, 710, -138);
    glVertex3f(-55, 710.0, -138);
    glVertex3f(-55, 730.0, -138);
    glEnd();

    //atas
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.86, 0.9, 0.56);
    glVertex3f(-135, 730, -138);
    glVertex3f(-135, 730, -65);
    glVertex3f(-55, 730.0, -65);
    glVertex3f(-55, 730.0, -138);
    glEnd();

    //kiri
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.86, 0.9, 0.56);
    glVertex3f(-135, 730, -138);
    glVertex3f(-135, 710, -138);
    glVertex3f(-135, 710, -65);
    glVertex3f(-135, 730, -65);
    glEnd();

    //kanan

void nGon(int r, int x, int y, int z) {
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    int sisi = 360;
    for (int i = 0; i < sisi; i++) {
        glVertex3f((r * cos(2 * 3.14159265 * i / sisi)) + x, (r * sin(2 * 3.14159265 * i / sisi) + y), z);
    }
    glEnd();
}

void patung() {
    //kepala
    //depan
    glPushMatrix();
    glTranslatef(-122.5, 0, 670);
    glBegin(GL_QUADS);

void pohon3(){
    // Kayu
   //depan
    glPushMatrix();
    glTranslatef(142, 0, 610.5);
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.2, 0.18, 0.12);
    glVertex3f(600, 0, 200);
    glVertex3f(650, 0, 200);
    glVertex3f(650, 150, 200);
    glVertex3f(600, 150, 200);
    glEnd();

    //belakang
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.2, 0.18, 0.12);
    glVertex3f(600, 0, 170);
    glVertex3f(650, 0, 170);
    glVertex3f(650, 150, 170);
    glVertex3f(600, 150, 170);
    glEnd();

    //kanan
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.2, 0.18, 0.12);
    glVertex3f(650, 0, 170);
    glVertex3f(650, 0, 200);
    glVertex3f(650, 150, 200);
    glVertex3f(650, 150, 170);
    glEnd();

    glVertex3f(520, 25, 270);
    glVertex3f(520, 25, 100);

    glVertex3f(500, 25, 270);

    glVertex3f(520, 25, 100);

}

void jalan_tangga() {
    //belakang

void pos() {
    //depan
    glPushMatrix();
    glTranslatef(-771, -20, 139);
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.96, 0.06, 0.06);
    glVertex3f(552, 100, 360);
    glVertex3f(552, 15, 360);
    glVertex3f(555, 15, 360);
    glVertex3f(555, 100, 360);
    glEnd();

    //belakang
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.96, 0.06, 0.06);
    glVertex3f(552, 15, 357);
    glVertex3f(552, 100, 357);
    glVertex3f(555, 100, 357);
    glVertex3f(555, 15, 357);
    glEnd();

    //kiri
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.96, 0.06, 0.06);
    glVertex3f(552, 100, 357);
    glVertex3f(552, 15, 357);
    glVertex3f(552, 15, 360);
    glVertex3f(552, 100, 360);
    glEnd();

    //kanan
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.96, 0.06, 0.06);
    glVertex3f(555, 100, 357);
    glVertex3f(555, 15, 357);
    glVertex3f(555, 15, 360);
    glVertex3f(555, 100, 360);
    glEnd();

    //atap
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.96, 0.06, 0.06);
    glVertex3f(530, 100, 345);
    glVertex3f(530, 100, 365);
    glVertex3f(575, 100, 365);
    glVertex3f(575, 100, 345);
    glEnd();

    //pos depan
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.96, 0.06, 0.06);
    glVertex3f(530, 150, 365);
    glVertex3f(530, 100, 365);
    glVertex3f(575, 100, 365);
    glVertex3f(575, 150, 365);
    glEnd();

    //pos belakang
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.96, 0.06, 0.06);
    glVertex3f(530, 150, 345);
    glVertex3f(530, 100, 345);
    glVertex3f(575, 100, 345);
    glVertex3f(575, 150, 345);
    glEnd();

    //pos kiri
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.96, 0.06, 0.06);
    glVertex3f(530, 100, 345);
    glVertex3f(530, 150, 345);
    glVertex3f(530, 150, 365);
    glVertex3f(530, 100, 365);
    glEnd();

    //pos kanan
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.96, 0.06, 0.06);
    glVertex3f(575, 150, 345);
    glVertex3f(575, 100, 345);
    glVertex3f(575, 100, 365);
    glVertex3f(575, 150, 365);
    glEnd();

    //pos atap
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.96, 0.06, 0.06);
    glVertex3f(530, 150, 365);
    glVertex3f(575, 150, 365);
    glVertex3f(575, 150, 345);
    glVertex3f(530, 150, 345);
    glEnd();

    //bolongankiri
    glPushMatrix();
    glTranslatef(-1.5, 0, 0);
    glPushMatrix();
    glTranslatef(-1, 0.5, 0);
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.13, 0.13, 0.13);
    glVertex3f(534, 145, 365.1);
    glVertex3f(534, 140, 365.1);
    glVertex3f(554, 140, 365.1);
    glVertex3f(554, 145, 365.1);
    glEnd();
    glPopMatrix();

    glPushMatrix();
    glTranslatef(0, 0.5, 0);
    glBegin(GL_TRIANGLES);
    glColor3f(0.43, 0.43, 0.41);
    glVertex3f(537, 145, 365.2);
    glVertex3f(548, 145, 365.2);
    glVertex3f(542.5, 142, 365.2);
    glEnd();
    glPopMatrix();
    glPopMatrix();
    //bolongankanan
    glPushMatrix();
    glTranslatef(20, 0, 0);
    glPushMatrix();
    glTranslatef(-1, 0.5, 0);
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.13, 0.13, 0.13);
    glVertex3f(534, 145, 365.1);
    glVertex3f(534, 140, 365.1);
    glVertex3f(554, 140, 365.1);
    glVertex3f(554, 145, 365.1);
    glEnd();
    glPopMatrix();

    glPushMatrix();

    glBegin(GL_TRIANGLES);
    glColor3f(0.43, 0.43, 0.41);
    glVertex3f(537, 145, 365.2);
    glVertex3f(548, 145, 365.2);
    glVertex3f(542.5, 142, 365.2);
    glEnd();
    glPopMatrix();
    glPopMatrix();
    glPopMatrix();
}

void lantai4() {
    glPushMatrix();
    glTranslatef(0, 365.5, 0);
    // depan
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.82, 0.78, 0.78);
    glVertex3f(-300, 320.0, 100);
    glVertex3f(-300, 300.0, 100);
    glVertex3f(105, 300.0, 100);
    glVertex3f(105, 320.0, 100);
    glEnd();

    // belakang
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.82, 0.78, 0.78);
    glVertex3f(-300, 320.0, -300);
    glVertex3f(-300, 300.0, -300);
    glVertex3f(105, 300.0, -300);
    glVertex3f(105, 320.0, -300);

    // atas
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.82, 0.78, 0.78);
    glVertex3f(-300, 320.0, -300);
    glVertex3f(-300, 320.0, 100);
    glVertex3f(105, 320.0, 100);
    glVertex3f(105, 320.0, -300);
    glEnd();

    // bawah
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.82, 0.78, 0.78);
    glVertex3f(-300, 300.1, -300);
    glVertex3f(-300, 300.1, 100);
    glVertex3f(105, 300.1, 100);
    glVertex3f(105, 300.1, -300);
    glEnd();

    // kiri
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.82, 0.78, 0.78);
    glVertex3f(-300, 320.0, -300);
    glVertex3f(-300, 300.0, -300);
    glVertex3f(-300, 300.0, 100);
    glVertex3f(-300, 320.0, 100);
    glEnd();

    // kanan
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.82, 0.78, 0.78);
    glVertex3f(105, 320.0, 100);
    glVertex3f(105, 300.0, 100);
    glVertex3f(105, 300.0, -300);
    glVertex3f(105, 320.0, -300);
    glEnd();
    glPopMatrix();

    // pagar 1 lantai 4
    // Bagian Depan
    glPushMatrix();
    glTranslatef(50, 365.5, -50);
    // atas
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.86, 0.39, 0);
    glVertex3f(-350.0, 390.0, 130);
    glVertex3f(-350.0, 390.0, 150);
    glVertex3f(40, 390.0, 150);
    glVertex3f(40, 390.0, 130);
    glEnd();

    // bawah
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.86, 0.39, 0);
    glVertex3f(-350.0, 380, 130);
    glVertex3f(-350.0, 380, 150);
    glVertex3f(40, 380, 150);
    glVertex3f(40, 380, 130);
    glEnd();

    // depan
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.86, 0.39, 0);
    glVertex3f(-350.0, 390.0, 150);// kiri atas
    glVertex3f(-350.0, 380.0, 150);// kiri bawah
    glVertex3f(40, 380.0, 150);// kanan bawah
    glVertex3f(40, 390.0, 150);// kanan atas
    glEnd();

    // belakang
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.86, 0.39, 0);
    glVertex3f(-350.0, 390.0, 130);// kiri atas
    glVertex3f(-350.0, 380.0, 130);// kiri bawah
    glVertex3f(40, 380.0, 130);// kanan bawah
    glVertex3f(40, 390.0, 130);// kanan atas
    glEnd();
    glPopMatrix();

    // Bagian Belakang 
    glPushMatrix();
    glTranslatef(50, 365.5, 50);
    // atas
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.86, 0.39, 0);
    glVertex3f(-350.0, 390.0, -350);
    glVertex3f(-350.0, 390.0, -340);
    glVertex3f(40, 390.0, -340);
    glVertex3f(40, 390.0, -350);
    glEnd();

    // bawah
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.86, 0.39, 0);

    glVertex3f(130.0, 320, -340);// kanan bawah
    glVertex3f(130.0, 390, -340);// kanan atas
    glEnd();

    //kanan
    glBegin(GL_POLYGON);
    glColor3f(0.86, 0.39, 0);
    glVertex3f(150.0, 390, -350);// kiri atas
    glVertex3f(150.0, 320, -350);// kiri bawah
    glVertex3f(150.0, 320, -340);// kanan bawah
    glVertex3f(150.0, 390, -340);// kanan atas
    glEnd();
    glPopMatrix();
}

void matahari() {
    int x = 0;
    int y = 100;
    glPushMatrix();
    glTranslatef(-537.5, 2198.5, 0);
    glColor4f(1, 0.95, 0.34, 0.2);
    for (x = 1; x <= 6; x++) {
        glutSolidSphere(y, 30, 30);
        y += 10;
    }
    glPopMatrix();
}

void display() {
    glClear(GL_COLOR_BUFFER_BIT | GL_DEPTH_BUFFER_BIT);
    glLoadIdentity();
    camera();
    draw();

    glutSwapBuffers();
}

void reshape(int w, int h) {
    glViewport(0, 0, w, h);
    glMatrixMode(GL_PROJECTION);
    glLoadIdentity();
    gluPerspective(50, 16.0 / 9.0, 2, 10000);
    glMatrixMode(GL_MODELVIEW);
}

void timer(int) {
    glutPostRedisplay();
    glutWarpPointer(width / 2, height / 2);
    glutTimerFunc(1000 / FPS, timer, 0);
}

void passive_motion(int x, int y) {
    int dev_x, dev_y;
    dev_x = (width / 2) - x;
    dev_y = (height / 2) - y;
    yaw += (float)dev_x / 20.0;
    pitch += (float)dev_y / 20.0;
}

void camera() {
    if (motion.Forward) {
        camX += cos((yaw + 90) * TO_RADIANS) * 2;
        camZ -= sin((yaw + 90) * TO_RADIANS) * 2;
    }
    if (motion.Backward) {
        camX += cos((yaw + 90 + 180) * TO_RADIANS) * 2;
        camZ -= sin((yaw + 90 + 180) * TO_RADIANS) * 2;
    }
    if (motion.Left) {
        camX += cos((yaw + 90 + 90) * TO_RADIANS) * 2;
        camZ -= sin((yaw + 90 + 90) * TO_RADIANS) * 2;
    }
    if (motion.Right) {
        camX += cos((yaw + 90 - 90) * TO_RADIANS) * 2;
        camZ -= sin((yaw + 90 - 90) * TO_RADIANS) * 2;
    }
    if (motion.Naik) {
        terbang -= 2.0;
    }
    if (motion.Turun) {
        terbang += 2.0;
    }

    if (pitch >= 70)
        pitch = 70;
    if (pitch <= -90)
        pitch = -90;


    glRotatef(-pitch, 1.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    glRotatef(-yaw, 0.0, 1.0, 0.0);

    glTranslatef(-camX, -terbang, -350 - camZ);
    if (terbang < 25)
        terbang = 24;
}

void keyboard(unsigned char key, int x, int y) {
    switch (key) {
    case 'W':
    case 'w':
        motion.Forward = true;
        break;
    case 'A':
    case 'a':
        motion.Left = true;
        break;
    case 'S':
    case 's':
        motion.Backward = true;
        break;
    case 'D':
    case 'd':
        motion.Right = true;
        break;
    case 'E':
    case 'e':
        motion.Naik = true;
        break;
    case 'Q':
    case 'q':
        motion.Turun = true;
        break;
    case '6':
        x_geser += 0.5;
        break;
    case '4':
        x_geser -= 0.5;
        break;
    case '8':
        y_geser += 0.5;
        break;
    case '2':
        y_geser -= 0.5;
        break;
    case '9':
        z_geser -= 0.5;
        break;
    case '1':
        z_geser += 0.5;
        break;
    case '`': // KELUAR DARI PROGRAM
        exit(1);
    }
}

void keyboard_up(unsigned char key, int x, int y) {
    switch (key) {
    case 'W':
    case 'w':
        motion.Forward = false;
        break;
    case 'A':
    case 'a':
        motion.Left = false;
        break;
    case 'S':
    case 's':
        motion.Backward = false;
        break;
    case 'D':
    case 'd':
        motion.Right = false;
        break;
    case 'E':
    case 'e':
        motion.Naik = false;
        break;
    case 'Q':
    case 'q':
        motion.Turun = false;
        break;
    }
}

int main(int argc, char** argv) {
    glutInit(&argc, argv);
    glutInitDisplayMode(GLUT_DOUBLE | GLUT_RGB | GLUT_DEPTH);
    glutInitWindowSize(width, height);
    glutCreateWindow("TR GRAFKOM KELOMPOK 2");

    init();
    glutDisplayFunc(display);
    glutReshapeFunc(reshape);
    glutPassiveMotionFunc(passive_motion);
    glutTimerFunc(0, timer, 0);
    glutKeyboardFunc(keyboard);
    glutKeyboardUpFunc(keyboard_up);

    glutMainLoop();
    return 0;
}
